Nikah — Marriage
intermediate
8 min
Marriage in Ihram: Valid but Disliked
Ruling with inter-madhhab dispute on marriage in ihram

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on marriage while in ihram, identify the key proofs from both sides, and explain the thamarah al-khilaf between the Hanafi and Shafi'i schools.

Core Idea
Marriage in ihram is valid but disliked (makruh tanzih) – the Hanafi position reconciles conflicting hadiths.

This passage addresses a well-known disagreement between the Hanafi and Shafi'i schools regarding the validity of marriage while a person is in the state of ihram. The Hanafi school, relying on the authentic hadith of Ibn Abbas that the Prophet married Maymunah while in ihram, holds that such a marriage is permissible but disliked. The Shafi'i school, citing the hadith of Uthman and a report from Maymunah herself, considers it invalid. The text reconciles the positions by concluding that marriage in ihram is makruh, not haram.

Guided Path
1
State the Hanafi position
Identify the ruling according to the Hanafi school: marriage while in ihram is permissible but makruh (disliked).
The text begins by stating it is jā'iz (permissible).
2
Identify the opponent and their proof
Imam al-Shafi'i holds that marriage in ihram is not permissible. His proofs: the hadith of Uthman ('The one in ihram should not marry...') and a report from Maymunah that the Prophet married her when he was halal.
The Shafi'i position is based on a different set of hadiths.
3
Analyze the Hanafi response
The Hanafis argue that the hadith of Ibn Abbas is authentic and takes precedence. They interpret the Shafi'i proofs as indicating karāha (dislike) not tahrīm (prohibition). The combination yields the ruling of makruh.
The key methodological principle: conflicting proofs are reconciled by jama', not by invalidating one.
4
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical consequence: Hanafis consider a marriage contracted in ihram valid (sahih) though disliked; Shafi'is consider it invalid (batil). If such a marriage occurs, Hanafis do not require a new contract, but Shafi'is do.
This is the real-world difference that matters for fatwa.
5
Note the tarjih
The author concludes that the Hanafi position is mufta bihi (relied upon for fatwa), based on the strength of the Ibn Abbas hadith and the principle of combining evidences.
The ruling is makruh tanzihī – disliked but not sinful.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
ويجوز للمحرم والمحرمة ان يتزوجا في حالة الاحرام [۱۷۵۲] (۲۷) اور جائز ہے محرم مرد اور محرمہ عورت کے لئے کہ دونوں شادی کریں احرام کی حالت میں۔
احرام کی حالت میں دونوں شادی کر دیں یہ جائز ہے۔
حدیث میں ہے کہ آپ نے حضرت میمونہ سے احرام کی حالت میں شادی کی تھی۔ انبانا ابن عباس تزوج النبي وهو محرم (الف) ( بخاری شریف، باب نکاح الحر م ص ۷۲۶ نمبر ۵۱۱۴ر مسلم شریف، باب تحریم نکاح محرم وكراهية خطبة ص۲۵۳ نمبر ۱۳۱۰ ترمذی شریف، نمبر ۸۴۲ را بو داؤد شریف، نمبر ۱۸۴۴) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ آپ نے احرام کی حالت میں حضرت میمونہ سے شادی کی ہے۔
نان امام شافعی فرماتے ہیں کہ احرام کی حالت میں شادی کرنا جائز نہیں ہے۔ ان کی دلیل یہ حدیث ہے۔ سمعت عثمان بن عفان يقول قال رسول الله لا ينكح المحرم ولا ينكح ولا يخطب (ب) (مسلم شریف، باب تحریم نکاح المحرم و کراهیه خطبته ص ۴۵۳ نمبر ۱۴۰۹ر ابو داؤد شریف، باب المحر م یتزوج ص۲۶۲ نمبر ۱۸۴۱) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ محرم شادی نہ کرے۔ اور حضرت میمونہ سے شادی کرنے کے بارے میں فرماتے ہیں کہ اس وقت آپ حلال تھے اور وہ اس حدیث سے استدلال کرتے ہیں۔ عن يزيد بن الاصم حدثتني ميمونة بنت الحارث ان رسول الله تزوجها وهو حلال (ج) (مسلم شریف ، باب تحریم نکاح المحرم و کراہیتہ خطبته ص ۴۵۳ نمبر ۱۴۱ ابوداؤد شریف، باب المحر م یتزوج ص۲۶۲ نمبر ۱۸۴۳ / ترندی شریف ، باب ماجاء فی کراہیتہ تزویج المحر م ص ۷۱ انمبر ۸۴۱) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ حضور حضرت میمونہ سے شادی کرتے وقت حلال تھے نوٹ احرام کی حالت میں نکاح مکروہ ہے۔ یہ دونوں حدیثوں کے مجموعے سے پتہ چلتا ہے۔ باکرہ اور شیبہ کے لئے ولی کے احکام کے
It is permissible for a man in ihram and a woman in ihram to marry each other in the state of ihram. [1752] (27) And it is permissible for a man in ihram and a woman in ihram that both marry in the state of ihram. It is permissible for both to marry in the state of ihram. In a hadith, it is mentioned that the Prophet married Maymunah while in the state of ihram. Ibn Abbas narrated: 'The Prophet married while he was in ihram.' (Bukhari, chapter on marriage of one in ihram, p. 726 no. 5114; Muslim, chapter on prohibition of marriage for one in ihram and dislike of proposing, p. 253 no. 1310; Tirmidhi no. 842; Abu Dawud no. 1844) This hadith indicates that the Prophet married Maymunah while in ihram. Now, Imam al-Shafi'i says that marriage in the state of ihram is not permissible. His proof is this hadith: 'Uthman ibn Affan said the Messenger of Allah said: 'The one in ihram should not marry, nor give in marriage, nor propose.' (Muslim, chapter on prohibition of marriage for one in ihram and dislike of proposing, p. 453 no. 1409; Abu Dawud, chapter on one in ihram marrying, p. 262 no. 1841) This hadith states that the one in ihram should not marry. Regarding the marriage to Maymunah, they say that at that time the Prophet was halal (not in ihram), and they argue from this hadith. From Yazid ibn al-Asamm: Maymunah bint al-Harith told me that the Messenger of Allah married her while he was halal. (Muslim, chapter on prohibition of marriage for one in ihram and dislike of proposing, p. 453 no. 141; Abu Dawud, chapter on one in ihram marrying, p. 262 no. 1843; Tirmidhi, chapter on dislike of marriage for one in ihram, p. 71 no. 841) This hadith shows that the Prophet was halal when he married Maymunah. Note: Marriage in the state of ihram is makruh. This is concluded from the combination of both hadiths.
Source pages p. 24

Commentary
This is an inter-madhhab dispute regarding marriage while in ihram. The Hanafi position, based on the hadith of Ibn Abbas, permits it, as the Prophet himself married Maymunah while in ihram. The Shafi'i position, based on the hadith of Uthman and a version from Maymunah herself, forbids it. The author reconciles by stating that marriage in ihram is makruh (disliked) rather than haram, given the conflicting evidence. The note indicates that the ruling is makruh, not absolutely forbidden.

Key Terms
محرم (muḥrim): A person who has entered the state of ihram for Hajj or Umrah.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the Hanafi ruling on a man in ihram marrying a woman?
A) Completely forbidden and invalid
B) Permissible and recommended
C) Valid but disliked (makruh)
D) Only allowed if the woman is also in ihram

Key Takeaway
Marriage in the state of ihram is valid (sahih) but disliked (makruh tanzih) according to the Hanafi school, based on combining the hadith of Ibn Abbas with the hadith of Uthman.
